## 19. Bridges teardown legacy вҖ” ~~defer pre-IVA-CRUD-hex-migration~~ **CLOSED post-POC siguiente**

Cuatro interfaces bridge IVA ~~quedan vivas post-POC #11.0c~~ **fueron teardown atГіmicamente en POC siguiente A1+A2** (bookmarks `poc-siguiente/a1/c2/closed` #1506 + `poc-siguiente/a2/c3/closed` #1514). El teardown era **pre-condiciГіn de cierre** del POC futuro que migre IVA CRUD a hex вҖ” POC siguiente entregГі esa pre-condiciГіn CUMPLIDA. (El bridge `SaleServiceForHub` queda fuera de В§19 вҖ” es SaleвҶ”Dispatch hub, defer atado a hub-migration POC, NO IVA-CRUD; cross-aggregate hidrataciГіn `Sale.period`/`displayCode`/`contact` permanece В§18.4 fila POC #11.0a contexto histГіrico.)

### 19.1. Interfaces afectadas

| Interface | Owner | Consumer | RazГіn shape-bound |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SaleServiceForBridge` (inbound IVAвҶ’Sale) | `features/sale/sale.service.ts` | `iva-books.service.ts:567 recomputeFromSaleCascade` | Contract requiere `externalTx` para atomicidad write-IVA + regen sale. В§5.5 retired Ciclo 6 elimina `externalTx` en hex `regenerateJournalForIvaChange` вҖ” el bridge no puede satisfacer la signature hex sin resucitar el path retirado. |
| `PurchaseServiceForBridge` (inbound IVAвҶ’Purchase) | `features/purchase/purchase.service.ts` | `iva-books.service.ts:626 recomputeFromPurchaseCascade` | Mirror simГ©trico sale-side (В§18.4 fila #11.0b A4 Оі). Misma shape-dependency `externalTx`. |
| `IvaBooksServiceForSaleCascade` (outbound SaleвҶ’IVA) | `features/accounting/iva-books/iva-books.service.ts` | `sale.service.ts:59 interface decl + 926 invocation en SaleService.editPosted` | Cascade `recomputeFromSaleCascade(tx, orgId, saleId, newTotal)` invocado desde `SaleService.editPosted` durante write-tx. Shape `tx`-bound legacy + path `regenerateJournalForIvaChange` (В§5.5 retired Ciclo 6). Re-rutear via puerto hex equivalente sin resucitar `externalTx` ni cross-tx coupling. |
| `IvaBooksServiceForPurchaseCascade` (outbound PurchaseвҶ’IVA) | `features/accounting/iva-books/iva-books.service.ts` | `purchase.service.ts:60 interface decl + 1078 invocation en PurchaseService.editPosted` | Mirror simГ©trico sale-side. Misma shape-dependency `tx`-bound + `regenerateJournalForIvaChange`. |

   - A1-C2: sale outbound asimetrГӯa (`IvaBooksServiceForSaleCascade`) deletion

В§18.4 fila POC nuevo dedicado A3 + В§19.6 status closure.

### 19.3. Por quГ© NO entra en В§15

В§15 lista pendientes iterables tras el POC `mortality` вҖ” items con scope no-bloqueante, refinables incrementalmente. Bridges teardown es **bloqueador estructural** pre-IVA-CRUD-hex-migration: condiciГіn binaria de cierre, no item refinable. Coherente con В§18 dejar la deuda explГӯcita con destino y forma de cierre conocidos (В§18.2 punto 4 вҖ” POC destino + acceptance del cierre).

### 19.4. Cross-ref

- **Origen**: В§18.4 fila POC #11.0c (Ві nota emergente A4-c) вҖ” defer lockeado D-Step0 Marco.
- **Engrams POC #11.0c**: `poc-11/0c/a4/c/closed` (P-items A4-c) вҖ” surface inicial blast radius bridges; `poc-11/0c/a4/closed` (POC #11.0c A4 entera CLOSED) вҖ” defer ratificado.

- **Complementa**: В§18 (caso simГ©trico forward вҖ” defer scope con destino conocido). В§19 es ejecuciГіn concreta de В§18 aplicada al cierre POC #11.0c вҖ” y POC siguiente es ejecuciГіn concreta del defer cumpliendo la pre-condiciГіn.

### 19.20. ADDENDUM POC correctivo dispatch-instantiation retroactivo bugfix build-blocking post-D1 poc-dispatch-hex

**ADDENDUM verify retroactivo POC correctivo dispatch-instantiation вҖ” build-blocking TSC regression detected post-D1 poc-dispatch-hex** (paired sister В§19.12 contacts correctivo RSC boundary precedent вҖ” instantiation axis distinct vs return-shape axis): `poc-dispatch-hex` C4 cutover commit `e3e6ad8b` switched `DispatchService` constructor to require `DispatchServiceDeps` arg (dependency injection). 7 consumer sites in `app/` were NOT updated вҖ” still calling `new DispatchService()` (zero-args form) post-cutover. `pnpm build` fails at TSC `Expected 1 arguments, but got 0` at `app/(dashboard)/[orgSlug]/dispatches/[dispatchId]/page.tsx:28` (first stop). Build-blocking debt hidden by repo rule "Never build after changes" вҖ” surfaced post-OLEADA 4 first build gate. Cascade TSC error also uncovered: `status/route.ts:37` called `dispatchService.void()` вҖ” method named `voidDispatch()` on `DispatchService`; fixed atomically in same file (declared consumer site, scope-bound).

**Root cause (instantiation axis)**: dependency injection via `DispatchServiceDeps` was added to `DispatchService` constructor during `poc-dispatch-hex` C4, but the 7 runtime consumer sites in `app/` import from the `server.ts` barrel which did NOT re-export `makeDispatchService()`. Factory existed in `modules/dispatch/presentation/composition-root.ts` but was unreachable from consumers. Fix: add barrel re-export (`server.ts` вҶ’ `./composition-root`) + replace all 7 `new DispatchService()` call sites with `makeDispatchService()`.

**4-commit chain (paired sister poc-correctivo-contacts precedent вҖ” instantiation axis variant)**:
- C0 RED `4a16c9a7` вҖ” `modules/dispatch/presentation/__tests__/c0-shape.poc-correctivo-dispatch-instantiation.test.ts` NEW 18Оұ sentinel gate (15 FAIL + 3 PASS-pre-existing at RED вҖ” mocks already had `makeDispatchService` key pre-C1a; Оұ16-Оұ18 PASS-locked)
- C1a mock-preceding `8386914f` вҖ” 3 vi.mock factory files verified already complete per [[mock_hygiene_commit_scope]] (no-op confirming state)
- C1b GREEN `2781c649` вҖ” 8-file atomic: `modules/dispatch/presentation/server.ts` barrel export + 7 consumer sites `new DispatchService()` вҶ’ `makeDispatchService()` + `status/route.ts` `void()` вҶ’ `voidDispatch()` cascade TSC fix
- C2 D1 (this commit) вҖ” doc-only В§19.20 ADDENDUM append-only

**REQ-005 NEGATIVE sentinel**: `new DispatchService()` (zero-args form) MUST NOT appear anywhere in `app/`. 18Оұ gate Оұ2+Оұ4+Оұ6+Оұ8+Оұ10+Оұ12+Оұ14 NEG per-site confirms zero-args form absent all 7 sites post-C1b. `pnpm build` advances past all dispatch TSC errors post-C1b (pre-existing cascade in `purchases/route.ts` MonetaryAmount type mismatch вҖ” separate module, out of scope).

**Scope (11 file edits total вҖ” per proposal В§2)**: `modules/dispatch/presentation/server.ts` (barrel) + 7 `app/` consumer sites (2 pages + 4 API routes + 1 hub route) + 3 test mock factory files. Suite: 18/18 Оұ PASS post-C1b. Full suite: 67 failed | 548 passed (baseline 68/547 вҖ” net improvement, 0 new failures; [[diagnostic_stash_gate_pattern]] confirmed page-rbac.test.ts P1001 Prisma + dispatches-hub/route.test.ts duplicate vi.mock collision both pre-existing). Duplicate vi.mock collapse OUT-OF-SCOPE per proposal В§2 вҖ” DEFER.
